	focus = {# Second Constitutional Convention
		id = CSA_second_convention

		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {

		}

			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus CSA_second_convention"

					}	
				}

			}

			}
			else_if = {

				}

			}
